For convenience and a good rest, I specifically chose a five-star hotel to stay in. I also made a special note in advance that there were elderly people.
You can check in after 14 o'clock. We arrived after 16 o'clock, but we said it hadn't been sorted out yet so we had to wait for almost an hour. The lady at the front desk was very responsible and kept going upstairs to urge us. So I didn't lose my temper because of this.
When I entered the room, I found that I was actually quite disappointed. Not to mention the outdated equipment and facilities, the overall layout was not considered a five-star hotel at all. Just put 2 bottles of water.
In other words, being close to the subway and attractions can alleviate my mother's bad mood.
Ordered takeout one night when I was really tired. The delivery guy said he needed to wait, but I said it was fine.
After waiting for almost 30 minutes, I went downstairs to pick it up. The staff in charge of the robot said that I had called the room three times. I was really drunk. I only called the room phone once to remind me to take out the food the day before yesterday, and I never used it again.
In short, I will not choose this hotel again when I come to Xi'an in the future.
The 4-point service is only given to the lady at the front desk, and the rest can only be said to be haha.

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Standard 2-bed Room
info:Stayed in July 2023
info:Family
info:1 Review

posted:Posted August 11, 2023
msg:Advantages: The hotel room is clean and tidy, the large bed and sofa are very comfortable, and the toiletries are L'Occitane brand. The air conditioner is very powerful on hot summer days. The hotel lobby is also very spacious and beautiful. The most important thing is that the hotel's location is very good. It is within the door-to-door pick-up and drop-off range for day tours, and you can also walk to the tour bus pick-up point in more than ten minutes. From the underground passage on the side of the hotel, you can walk to the clock tower. The hotel is also not far from the subway station. Another advantage is that although it is located in the city center, the hotel is not facing the street, so it is very quiet. There are several great restaurants within a few dozen meters of the hotel. There is also a 24-hour convenience store.

Disadvantages: The sliding door of the hotel toilet is a safety hazard. It should be changed to a push-open door. It is recommended not to pull the sliding door all the way and close it completely. In addition, the hotel fully meets the five-star conditions.

posted:Posted August 6, 2023
msg:The first time I went to Xi'an was 10 years ago. In my memory, the hotel closest to the bustling area and impressive was the Imperial City. I guess I was attracted by the name at the timeüòä
There is a drinking area for sour plum soup and barley tea at the entrance of the hotel. At the end of the day, you can have a cup of sour plum soup, which is both thirst-quenching and delicious. The hotel's breakfast is rich in variety and satisfies your energy intake.
It's an old hotel. The rooms are small and the facilities are old, but overall it's tidy. When I come back every day, the toiletries are replenished. The room has a small balcony. It's cold in Xi'an in the morning and evening. I can sit on the balcony for a while in the morning and evening and drink some tea. It's very nice. Comfortable.
The transportation near the hotel is very convenient. There is a bus stop right outside the door and the subway is just a few steps away. It is very convenient to go to any attractions.
The second time I went there, I felt that the prosperous areas in Xi'an have gradually moved to the vicinity of the Tang Dynasty Sleepless City. This place is no longer as prosperous as it used to be~
I wish Xi'an will get better and better, and I will go there again if I have the opportunity...
